  13→// limitations under the License.\n    14→\n    15→package v3compactor\n    16→\n    17→import (\n    18→\t\"context\"\n    19→\t\"errors\"\n    20→\t\"sync\"\n    21→\t\"time\"\n    22→\n    23→\t\"github.com/jonboulle/clockwork\"\n    24→\t\"go.uber.org/zap\"\n    25→\n    26→\tpb \"go.etcd.io/etcd/api/v3/etcdserverpb\"\n    27→\t\"go.etcd.io/etcd/server/v3/storage/mvcc\"\n    28→)\n    29→\n    30→// Periodic compacts the log by purging revisions older than\n    31→// the configured retention time.\n    32→type Periodic struct {\n    33→\tlg     *zap.Logger\n    34→\tclock  clockwork.Clock\n    35→\tperiod time.Duration\n    36→\n    37→\trg RevGetter\n    38→\tc  Compactable\n    39→\n    40→\trevs   []int64\n    41→\tctx    context.Context\n    42→\tcancel context.CancelFunc\n    43→\n    44→\t// mu protects paused\n    45→\tmu     sync.RWMutex\n    46→\tpaused bool\n    47→}\n    48→\n    49→// newPeriodic creates a new instance of Periodic compactor that purges\n    50→// the log older than h Duration.\n    51→func newPeriodic(lg *zap.Logger, clock clockwork.Clock, h time.Duration, rg RevGetter, c Compactable) *Periodic {\n    52→\tpc := &Periodic{\n    53→\t\tlg:     lg,\n    54→\t\tclock:  clock,\n    55→\t\tperiod: h,\n    56→\t\trg:     rg,\n    57→\t\tc:      c,\n    58→\t}\n    59→\t// revs won't be longer than the retentions.\n    60→\tpc.revs = make([]int64, 0, pc.getRetentions())\n    61→\tpc.ctx, pc.cancel = context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n    62→\treturn pc\n    63→}\n    64→\n    65→/*\n    66→Compaction period 1-hour:\n    67→  1. compute compaction period, which is 1-hour\n    68→  2. record revisions for every 1/10 of 1-hour (6-minute)\n    69→  3. keep recording revisions with no compaction for first 1-hour\n    70→  4. do compact with revs[0]\n    71→\t- success? continue on for-loop and move sliding window; revs = revs[1:]\n    72→\t- failure? update revs, and retry after 1/10 of 1-hour (6-minute)\n    73→\n    74→Compaction period 24-hour:\n    75→  1. compute compaction period, which is 24-hour\n    76→  2. record revisions for every 1/10 of 24-hour (144-minute)\n    77→  3. keep recording revisions with no compaction for first 24-hour\n    78→  4. do compact with revs[0]\n    79→\t- success? continue on for-loop and move sliding window; revs = revs[1:]\n    80→\t- failure? update revs, and retry after 1/10 of 24-hour (144-minute)\n    81→\n    82→Compaction period 59-min:\n    83→  1. compute compaction period, which is 59-min\n    84→  2. record revisions for every 1/10 of 59-min (5.9-min)\n    85→  3. keep recording revisions with no compaction for first 59-min\n    86→  4. do compact with revs[0]\n    87→\t- success? continue on for-loop and move sliding window; revs = revs[1:]\n    88→\t- failure? update revs, and retry after 1/10 of 59-min (5.9-min)\n    89→\n    90→Compaction period 5-sec:\n    91→  1. compute compaction period, which is 5-sec\n    92→  2. record revisions for every 1/10 of 5-sec (0.5-sec)\n    93→  3. keep recording revisions with no compaction for first 5-sec\n    94→  4. do compact with revs[0]\n    95→\t- success? continue on for-loop and move sliding window; revs = revs[1:]\n    96→\t- failure? update revs, and retry after 1/10 of 5-sec (0.5-sec)\n    97→*/\n    98→\n    99→// Run runs periodic compactor.\n   100→func (pc *Periodic) Run() {\n   101→\tcompactInterval := pc.getCompactInterval()\n   102→\tretryInterval := pc.getRetryInterval()\n   103→\tretentions := pc.getRetentions()\n   104→\n   105→\tgo func() {\n   106→\t\tlastRevision := int64(0)\n   107→\t\tlastSuccess := pc.clock.Now()\n   108→\t\tbaseInterval := pc.period\n   109→\t\tfor {\n   110→\t\t\tpc.revs = append(pc.revs, pc.rg.Rev())\n   111→\t\t\tif len(pc.revs) > retentions {\n   112→\t\t\t\tpc.revs = pc.revs[1:] // pc.revs[0] is always the rev at pc.period ago\n   113→\t\t\t}\n   114→\n   115→\t\t\tselect {\n   116→\t\t\tcase <-pc.ctx.Done():\n   117→\t\t\t\treturn\n   118→\t\t\tcase <-pc.clock.After(retryInterval):\n   119→\t\t\t\tpc.mu.RLock()\n   120→\t\t\t\tp := pc.paused\n   121→\t\t\t\tpc.mu.RUnlock()\n   122→\t\t\t\tif p {\n   123→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   124→\t\t\t\t}\n   125→\t\t\t}\n   126→\t\t\trev := pc.revs[0]\n   127→\t\t\tif pc.clock.Now().Sub(lastSuccess) < baseInterval || rev == lastRevision It enables quick\n// events look up by watcher.\nfunc newWatcherBatch(wg *watcherGroup, evs []mvccpb.Event) watcherBatch {\n\tif len(wg.watchers) == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\twb := make(watcherBatch)\n\tfor _, ev := range evs {\n\t\tfor w := range wg.watcherSetByKey(string(ev.Kv.Key)) {\n\t\t\tif ev.Kv.ModRevision >= w.minRev {\n\t\t\t\t// don't double notify\n\t\t\t\twb.add(w, ev)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn wb\n}\n\ntype watcherSet map[*watcher]struct{}\n\nfunc (w watcherSet) add(wa *watcher) {\n\tif _, ok := w[wa]; !ok {\n\t\tpanic(\"removing missing watcher!\")\n\t}\n\tdelete(w, wa)\n}\n\ntype watcherSetByKey map[string]watcherSet\n\nfunc (w watcherSetByKey) add(wa *watcher) {\n\tset := w[string(wa.key)]\n\tif set == nil {\n\t\tset = make(watcherSet)\n\t\tw[string(wa.key)] = set\n\t}\n\tset.add(wa)\n}\n\nfunc (w watcherSetByKey) delete(wa *watcher) bool {\n\tk := string(wa.key)\n\tif v, ok := w[k]; it is sorted by interval\n\tranges adt.IntervalTree\n\t// watchers is the set of all watchers\n\twatchers watcherSet\n}\n\nfunc newWatcherGroup() watcherGroup {\n\treturn watcherGroup{\n\t\tkeyWatchers: make(watcherSetByKey),\n\t\tranges:      adt.NewIntervalTree(),\n\t\twatchers:    make(watcherSet),\n\t}\n}\n\n// add puts a watcher in the group.\nfunc (wg *watcherGroup) add(wa *watcher) {\n\twg.watchers.add(wa)\n\tif wa.end == nil {\n\t\twg.keyWatchers.add(wa)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// interval already registered?\n\tivl := adt.NewStringAffineInterval(string(wa.key), string(wa.end))\n\tif iv := wg.ranges.Find(ivl); etcd\\n\\n### 1. Compaction Schedule (Periodic vs Revision-based)\\n\\nThe compaction schedule is defined in `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/`:\\n\\n- **compactor.go** (lines 28-73): Defines the `Compactor` interface with `Run()`, `Stop()`, `Pause()`, `Resume()` methods. The `New()` factory function creates either a periodic or revision-based compactor based on mode parameter. Also defines `Compactable` and `RevGetter` interfaces that the store must implement.\\n\\n- **periodic.go** (lines 32-209): Implements `Periodic` compactor that uses a retention duration. The `Run()` method (lines 100-163) implements a sliding window algorithm: records revisions every 1/10th of the retention period, waits for the full retention period to elapse, then performs compaction on the oldest revision. Uses clockwork for time management and supports pause/resume.\\n\\n- **revision.go** (lines 32-131): Implements `Revision` compactor that compacts based on revision count. The `Run()` method (lines 65-112) runs every 5 minutes (revInterval at line 62) and compacts revisions older than the retention count from the current revision.\\n\\n### 2. Compaction of Revision Indices\\n\\nThe core compaction logic operates on revision indices:\\n\\n- **kvstore.go** (lines 271-283): The main `Compact()` method is the entry point. It checks if previous compaction is completed, updates the compact revision via `updateCompactRev()` (lines 196-221), then schedules the actual compaction via `compact()` (lines 233-259). Uses a FIFO scheduler to execute compaction asynchronously and returns a channel that signals completion.\\n\\n- **kvstore_compaction.go** (lines 28-100): The `scheduleCompaction()` function implements the physical compaction. It compacts the key index via `kvindex.Compact()` to determine which revisions to keep. Then iterates through the database in batches, deletes keys marked for compaction, computes a hash, and calls `UnsafeSetFinishedCompact()` to persist the finished compact revision. Uses metrics to track compaction duration and key counts.\\n\\n- **index.go** (line 192): The `treeIndex.Compact()` method returns a map of revisions to keep based on the compaction revision.\\n\\n- **key_index.go** (line 258): The `keyIndex.doCompact()` method removes old generation entries from the key index.\\n\\n- **store.go** (lines 22-56): Provides safe access to scheduled/finished compact revision metadata in the backend via `UnsafeReadScheduledCompact()`, `UnsafeReadFinishedCompact()`, and the unsafe setters.\\n\\n### 3. For each watcher in a group, if `watcher.minRev < compactRev` (line 251), it sends a `WatchResponse` with `CompactRevision` set to the compact revision and `compacted` flag set to true (lines 252-254). The watcher is then removed from the group.\\n\\n- **watcher.go** (lines 82-98): Defines `WatchResponse` struct with `CompactRevision` field (line 97) that is set when the watcher is cancelled due to compaction. Also defines the `WatchStream` interface for managing watchers.\\n\\n- **watchable_store.go** (lines 341-414): The `syncWatchers()` method (lines 346-414) calls `s.unsynced.choose()` with the current `compactionRev` (line 363). The choose method determines which watchers span the compacted region and sends them the CompactRevision notification.\\n\\n- **api/v3rpc/watch.go** (lines 458-465): The RPC layer handles the CompactRevision in watch responses. When `wresp.CompactRevision != 0` (line 458), it sets `canceled` to true and includes the `CompactRevision` in the gRPC `WatchResponse` (line 463).\\n\\n### 4. Slow Watch Detection\\n\\nWatchers that fall behind the current revision are tracked as \\\"slow\\\":\\n\\n- **watchable_store.go** (lines 127-157): In the `watch()` method, when `startRev <= s.store.currentRev` (meaning the watch starts from a past revision), the watcher is added to the unsynced group and `slowWatcherGauge.Inc()` is called (line 148) to track it as a slow watcher.\\n\\n- **watchable_store.go** (lines 411): In `syncWatchers()`, the slow watcher gauge is updated to reflect the total count of unsynced watchers plus victim watchers: `slowWatcherGauge.Set(float64(s.unsynced.size() + vsz))`.\\n\\n- **watchable_store.go** (lines 164, 191, 324): When slow watchers are moved to synced state or removed, `slowWatcherGauge.Dec()` is called to decrement the count.\\n\\n- **metrics.go** (lines 87-94): Defines `slowWatcherGauge` as a Prometheus gauge metric under the `etcd_debugging` namespace, tracking \\\"Total number of unsynced slow watchers\\\".\\n\\n### Integration Flow\\n\\nWhen a compaction is triggered:\\n\\n1. The `Periodic` or `Revision` compactor calls the server's `Compact()` method\\n2. Server processes it through the RPC layer (`v3_server.go`) and apply infrastructure\\n3. Apply backend (`apply/backend.go`) calls `kv.Compact()` on the KV store\\n4. The store's `Compact()` method updates the compact revision and schedules `scheduleCompaction()`\\n5. Compaction deletes old keys and updates the finished compact revision\\n6. When `syncWatchers()` is called on the watchable store, it gets watchers from unsynced group and calls `choose()` with the compact revision\\n7. `watcher_group.chooseAll()` sends CompactRevision notifications to slow watchers whose minRev < compactRev\\n8. Slow Watch Detection\\n\\nWatchers that fall behind the current revision are tracked as \\\"slow\\\":\\n\\n- **watchable_store.go** (lines 127-157): In the `watch()` method, when `startRev <= s.store.currentRev` (meaning the watch starts from a past revision), the watcher is added to the unsynced group and `slowWatcherGauge.Inc()` is called (line 148) to track it as a slow watcher.\\n\\n- **watchable_store.go** (lines 411): In `syncWatchers()`, the slow watcher gauge is updated to reflect the total count of unsynced watchers plus victim watchers: `slowWatcherGauge.Set(float64(s.unsynced.size() + vsz))`.\\n\\n- **watchable_store.go** (lines 164, 191, 324): When slow watchers are moved to synced state or removed, `slowWatcherGauge.Dec()` is called to decrement the count.\\n\\n- **metrics.go** (lines 87-94): Defines `slowWatcherGauge` as a Prometheus gauge metric under the `etcd_debugging` namespace, tracking \\\"Total number of unsynced slow watchers\\\".\\n\\n### Integration Flow\\n\\nWhen a compaction is triggered:\\n\\n1. The `Periodic` or `Revision` compactor calls the server's `Compact()` method\\n2. Server processes it through the RPC layer (`v3_server.go`) and apply infrastructure\\n3. Apply backend (`apply/backend.go`) calls `kv.Compact()` on the KV store\\n4. The store's `Compact()` method updates the compact revision and schedules `scheduleCompaction()`\\n5. Compaction deletes old keys and updates the finished compact revision\\n6. When `syncWatchers()` is called on the watchable store, it gets watchers from unsynced group and calls `choose()` with the compact revision\\n7. `watcher_group.chooseAll()` sends CompactRevision notifications to slow watchers whose minRev < compactRev\\n8. The RPC layer sends these notifications to clients via gRPC watch responses\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
